---
about_this_resource_text: "<p><strong>Description:</strong> The study of sound textures\
  \ and high level goals of auditory processing. Anatomy and structure of the auditory\
  \ system, frequency tuning of cochlear transduction, perception of real-world textures\
  \ using synthesized textures with similar statistics.</p>\r\n<p><strong>Instructor:</strong>\
  \ Josh McDermott</p>"

  <span m='2260050'>about</span> <span m='2260260'>exactly</span> <span m='2260620'>what's</span>
  <span m='2260770'>happening</span> <span m='2261070'>in</span> <span m='2261130'>the</span>
  <span m='2261220'>waveform,</span> <span m='2261640'>namely,</span> <span m='2262240'>you</span>
  <span m='2262690'>know</span> <span m='2262930'>that</span> <span m='2263050'>there's</span>
  <span m='2263830'>energy</span> <span m='2264190'>there</span> <span m='2264580'>in</span>
  <span m='2264970'>the</span> <span m='2265060'>stimulus</span> <span m='2265420'>because</span>
  <span m='2265660'>you're</span> <span m='2265750'>getting</span> <span m='2265990'>spikes,</span>
  <span m='2266720'>but</span> <span m='2266800'>you</span> <span m='2266860'>also</span>
  <span m='2267190'>actually</span> <span m='2267430'>know</span> <span m='2267550'>the</span>
  <span m='2267670'>phase</span> <span m='2268000'>of</span> <span m='2268120'>the</span>
  <span m='2268210'>waveform</span> <span m='2268660'>because</span> <span m='2269230'>the</span>
  <span m='2269530'>spikes</span> <span m='2269800'>are</span> <span m='2269860'>happening</span>
  <span m='2270190'>in</span> <span m='2270280'>particular</span> <span m='2270730'>places.</span>
  </p><p><span m='2272740'>And</span> <span m='2273610'>so</span> <span m='2274250'>this</span>
  <span m='2274510'>issue</span> <span m='2274780'>of</span> <span m='2274870'>phase</span>
  <span m='2275290'>is</span> <span m='2275380'>sort</span> <span m='2275560'>of</span>
  <span m='2275650'>a</span> <span m='2275710'>tricky</span> <span m='2276040'>one,</span>
  <span m='2276550'>because</span> <span m='2276760'>it's</span> <span m='2276880'>often</span>

  <span m='2277660'>we</span> <span m='2277750'>really</span> <span m='2277960'>know</span>

  </p><p><span m='2292420'>And</span> <span m='2292510'>so</span> <span m='2292630'>the</span>

  <span m='2454630'>want to</span> <span m='2454690'>synthesize</span> <span m='2455170'>a</span>

  <span m='2455860'>usually</span> <span m='2456040'>what</span> <span m='2456160'>we</span>

  <span m='2462940'>we</span> <span m='2463060'>split</span> <span m='2463360'>it</span>
  <span m='2463450'>up</span> <span m='2463570'>into</span> <span m='2463910'>its</span>
  <span m='2464190'>subbands.</span> </p><p><span m='2465610'>And</span> <span m='2465760'>then</span>

  <span m='2467830'>noise</span> <span m='2468270'>subbands</span> <span m='2469000'>by</span>

  <span m='2470140'>this</span> <span m='2470290'>picture.</span> <span m='2471190'>OK?</span>

  <span m='3434920'>in</span> <span m='3434980'>this</span> <span m='3435130'>matrix</span>
  <span m='3435610'>here.</span> <span m='3436240'>So</span> <span m='3436390'>every</span>
  <span m='3436630'>cell</span> <span m='3436930'>of</span> <span m='3437380'>this</span>
  <span m='3437500'>matrix</span> <span m='3437950'>is</span> <span m='3438100'>the</span>

  <span m='3632060'>walk</span> <span m='3632430'>you through the</span> <span m='3632540'>logic.</span>
